saṃkṣepeṇa paśyet vyavalokayet granthato rthato vā atrāpi pūrvakameva prayojanam  yadi vāBcp  āryanāgārjunābaddhaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca prayatnataḥ  Bca āryanāgārjunapādairnibaddhaṃ dvitīyaṃ śikṣāsamuccayaṃ vidhīyatetat prasiddhaṃ vihitaṃ vā lokānāṃ cittamāśayaḥ tasya rakṣārthamtadyathā vikopitaṃ na syāt śikṣāṃ dṛṣṭvā śikṣāsamuccayādiṣu pratipādaṃ samācaretyatra yadyathā yujyatetatra tathā vyavaharet niṣpatsyatetāvanmātreṇa rogasya tasyāvinivṛtteḥ na kiṃciditi bhāvaḥ tasmāt sarvametat kriyānuṣṭhānena niṣpādayitavyamiti iti prajñākaramativiracitāyāṃ bodhicaryāvatārapañjikāyāṃ saṃprajanyarakṣaṇaṃ nāma pañcamaḥ paricchedaḥ Bcp  kṣāntipāramitā nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ paricchedaḥ tadevaṃ bahudhā śīlaviśuddhiṃ pratipādya ātmabhāvādīnāṃ rakṣāṃ śuddhiṃ pratipādya śubhaviśuddhiṃ pratipādayitum yaccoktamkṣameta kalpasahasrairyatpratighaḥ pratihanti tat  Bca sarvametaditi śīlasaṃvarasamādānaprasūtam sucaritaṃ kuśalaṃ karma dānaṃ trividham sāmānyena sugatapūjanamapi trividham kṛtam upārjitamanekaiḥ vividhairnānāprakārairupāyairvakṣyamāṇaiḥ Bcp  dṛṣṭadharma eva dveṣasya doṣān vṛttatrayeṇopadarśayannāhamanaḥ śamaṃ na gṛhṇāti na prītisukhamaśrute na nidrāṃ na dhṛtiṃ yāti dveṣaśalye hṛdi sthite  Bca pūjayatyarthamānauryān ye pi cainaṃ samāśritāḥ te pyanaṃ hantumicchanti svāminaṃ dveṣadurbhagam  Bca suhṛdo pyudvijante smād dadāti na ca sevyate saṃkṣepānnāsti tatkiṃcit krodhano yena susthitaḥ  Bca śamaṃ praśamaṃ na gṛhṇāti nāśrayate anupaśānta eva sadā dveṣānalaprajvalitatvāt na prītisukhaṃ saumanasyasukhamaśnute āpnotitenaivākrāntatvāt na nidrāṃ na dhṛtiṃ cittasukhaṃ labhate
